style="width:22em">\n       <tr>\n        <th class="summary" colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">\n         <i>\n          Endeavour\n          <br/>\n          OV-105\n         </i>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-127_Launch_Pad_39A.jpg">\n          <img alt="STS-127 Launch Pad 39A.jpg" data-file-height="3000" data-file-width="2008" height="329" <i>\n           Endeavour\n          </i>\n          on\n          <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center_Launch_Complex_39#LC-39A" title="Kennedy Space Center Launch Complex 39">\n           launch pad 39A\n          </a>\n          prior to mission\n          <a href="/wiki/STS-127" title="STS-127">\n           STS-127\n          </a>\n          , May 31, 2009\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Vehicle_Designation" title="Orbiter Vehicle Designation">\n          OV designation\n         </a>\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         OV-105\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Country\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         United States\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Contract award\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         July 31, 1987\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Named after\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/HMS_Endeavour" title="HMS Endeavour">\n          HMS\n          <i>\n           Endeavour\n          </i>\n         </a>\n         (1764)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Status\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         Retired, displayed at\n         <a href="/wiki/California_Science_Center" title="California Science Center">\n          California Science Center\n         </a>\n         in\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Los_Angeles,_California" title="Los Angeles, California">\n          Los Angeles, California\n         </a>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         First flight\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/STS-49" title="STS-49">\n          STS-49\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         May 7, 1992 \xe2\x80\x93 May 16, 1992\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Last flight\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/STS-134" title="STS-134">\n          STS-134\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         May 16, 2011 - June 1, 2011\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         <abbr title="Number">\n          No.\n         </abbr>\n         of missions\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         25\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Crew members\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         173\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Time spent in space\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         296 days, 3 hours, 34 minutes, 2 seconds\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         <abbr title="Number">\n          No.\n         </abbr>\n         of orbits\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         4,671\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Distance travelled\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         122,883,151\xc2\xa0mi (197,761,262\xc2\xa0km)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Satellites deployed\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         3\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         <a href="/wiki/Mir" title="Mir">\n          Mir\n         </a>\n         dockings\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         1\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n          ISS\n         </a>\n         dockings\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         12\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        Space Shuttle\n        <i>\n         Endeavour\n        </i>\n       </b>\n       (\n       <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Vehicle_Designation" title="Orbiter Vehicle Designation">\n        Orbiter Vehicle Designation\n       </a>\n       :\n       <b>\n        OV-105\n       </b>\n       ) is a retired\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_orbiter" title="Space Shuttle orbiter">\n        orbiter\n       </a>\n       from\n       <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">\n        NASA\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_program" title="Space Shuttle program">\n        Space Shuttle program\n       </a>\n       and the fifth and final operational\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle" title="Space Shuttle">\n        shuttle\n       </a>\n       built. It embarked on its first mission,\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-49" title="STS-49">\n        STS-49\n       </a>\n       , in May 1992 and its 25th and final mission,\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-134" title="STS-134">\n        STS-134\n       </a>\n       , in May 2011.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       STS-134 was expected to be the final mission of the Space Shuttle program,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       but with the authorization of\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-135" title="STS-135">\n        STS-135\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Atlantis" title="Space Shuttle Atlantis">\n        <i>\n         Atlantis\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       became the last shuttle to fly.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">\n        United States Congress\n       </a>\n       approved the construction of\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       in 1987 to replace\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Challenger" title="Space Shuttle Challenger">\n        <i>\n         Challenger\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       , which was\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Challenger_disaster" title="Space Shuttle Challenger disaster">\n        lost in 1986\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Structural spares built during the construction of\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Discovery" title="Space Shuttle Discovery">\n         Discovery\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       and\n       <i>\n        Atlantis\n       </i>\n       were used in its assembly. NASA chose, on cost grounds, to build\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       from spares rather than refitting\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Enterprise" title="Space Shuttle Enterprise">\n         Enterprise\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       or accepting a\n       <a href="/wiki/Rockwell_International" title="Rockwell International">\n        Rockwell International\n       </a>\n       proposal to build two shuttles for the price of one.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toc" id="toc">\n       <div class="toctitle">\n  </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-10">\n         <a href="#California_Science_Center">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           6\n          </span>\n          <span    as photographed from the\n         <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n          International Space Station\n         </a>\n         as it approached  <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Endeavour_silhouette_STS-130.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <i>\n          Endeavour\n         </i>\n         appears to straddle the\n         <a href="/wiki/Stratosphere" title="Stratosphere">\n          stratosphere\n         </a>\n         and\n         <a href="/wiki/Mesosphere" International Space Station\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The orbiter is named after the British\n       <a href="/wiki/HMS_Endeavour" title="HMS Endeavour">\n        HMS\n        <i>\n         Endeavour\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       , the ship which took Captain\n       <a href="/wiki/James_Cook" title="James Cook">\n        James Cook\n       </a>\n       on his\n       <a href="/wiki/First_voyage_of_James_Cook" title="First voyage of James Cook">\n        first voyage\n       </a>\n       of discovery (1768\xe2\x80\x931771).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This is why the name is spelled in the\n       <a href="/wiki/British_English" title="British English">\n        British English\n       </a>\n       manner, rather than the\n       <a href="/wiki/American_English" title="American English">\n        American English\n       </a>\n       ("Endeavor"). This has caused confusion, including when NASA itself misspelled a sign on the launch pad in 2007.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-spellingoops_6-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-spellingoops-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Space Shuttle carried a piece of the original wood from Cook\xe2\x80\x99s ship inside the cockpit.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The name also honored\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Apollo_Command/Service_Module" title="Apollo Command/Service Module">\n        Command Module\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a href="/wiki/Apollo_15" title="Apollo 15">\n        Apollo 15\n       </a>\n       , which was also named after Cook\'s ship.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       was named through a national competition involving students in elementary and secondary schools. Entries included an essay about the name, the story behind it and why it was appropriate for a NASA shuttle, and the project that supported the name.\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       was the most popular entry, accounting for almost one-third of the state-level winners. The national winners were Senatobia Middle School in\n       <a href="/wiki/Senatobia,_Mississippi" title="Senatobia, Mississippi">\n        Senatobia, Mississippi\n       </a>\n       , in the elementary division and\n       <a href="/wiki/Tallulah_Falls_School" title="Tallulah Falls School">\n        Tallulah Falls School\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Tallulah_Falls,_Georgia" title="Tallulah Falls, Georgia">\n        Tallulah Falls, Georgia\n       </a>\n       , in the upper school division. They were honored at several ceremonies in Washington, D.C., including a White House ceremony where then-President\n       <a href="/wiki/George_H._W._Bush" title="George H. W. Bush">\n        George H. W. Bush\n       </a>\n       presented awards to each school.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa.gov_8-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nasa.gov-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       was delivered by\n       <a href="/wiki/Rockwell_International" title="Rockwell International">\n        Rockwell International\n       </a>\n       Space Transportation Systems Division in May 1991 and first launched a year later, in May 1992, on\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-49" title="STS-49">\n        STS-49\n       </a>\n       . Rockwell International claimed that it had made no profit on Space Shuttle\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       , despite construction costing US$2.2\xc2\xa0billion.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2015)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Service">\n        Service\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Space_Shuttle_Endeavour&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Service">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       On its first mission, it captured and redeployed the stranded\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Intelsat" title="Intelsat">\n         INTELSAT\n        </a>\n        VI\n       </i>\n       communications satellite. The first African-American woman astronaut,\n       <a href="/wiki/Mae_Jemison" title="Mae Jemison">\n        Mae Jemison\n       </a>\n       , was launched into space on the mission\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-47" title="STS-47">\n        STS-47\n       </a>\n       on September 12, 1992.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       flew the first servicing mission\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-61" title="STS-61">\n        STS-61\n       </a>\n       for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hubble_Space_Telescope" title="Hubble Space Telescope">\n        Hubble Space Telescope\n       </a>\n       in 1993. In 1997 it was withdrawn from service for eight months for a retrofit, including installation of a new airlock. In December 1998, it delivered the\n       <a href="/wiki/Unity_(ISS_module)" title="Unity (ISS module)">\n        Unity Module\n       </a>\n       to the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\'\n       </i>\n       s last Orbiter Major Modification period began in December 2003 and ended on October 6, 2005. During this time,\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       received major hardware upgrades, including a new, multi-functional, electronic display system, often referred to as a\n       <a href="/wiki/Glass_cockpit" title="Glass cockpit">\n        glass cockpit\n       </a>\n       , and an advanced\n       <a href="/wiki/Global_Positioning_System" title="Global Positioning System">\n        GPS\n       </a>\n       receiver, along with safety upgrades recommended by the\n       <a href="/wiki/Columbia_Accident_Investigation_Board" title="Columbia Accident Investigation Board">\n        Columbia Accident Investigation Board\n       </a>\n       (CAIB) for the shuttle\'s return to flight following the\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Columbia_disaster" title="Space Shuttle Columbia disaster">\n        loss of\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Columbia" title="Space Shuttle Columbia">\n        <i>\n         Columbia\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       during reentry on 1 February 2003.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-118" title="STS-118">\n        STS-118\n       </a>\n       mission,\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\'\n       </i>\n       s first since the refit, included astronaut\n       <a href="/wiki/Barbara_Morgan" title="Barbara Morgan">\n        Barbara Morgan\n       </a>\n       , formerly assigned to the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Teacher_in_Space_project" title="Teacher in Space project">\n        Teacher in Space project\n       </a>\n       , but now a full member of the Astronaut Corps, as part of the crew. Morgan was the backup for\n       <a href="/wiki/Christa_McAuliffe" title="Christa McAuliffe">\n        Christa McAuliffe\n       </a>\n       who was on the ill-fated mission\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-51-L" title="STS-51-L">\n        STS-51-L\n       </a>\n       in 1986.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Early_milestones">\n        Early milestones\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a      ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table border="1" class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th style="background:#efefef;">\n         Date\n        </th>\n        <th     [10]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         1987 July 31\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Contract award to\n         <a title="STS-49">\n          STS-49\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Upgrades_and_features">\n        Upgrades and features\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Space_Shuttle_Endeavour&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Upgrades and features">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Space_Shuttle_Transit.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1520" data-file-width="2268" height="147"  mounted on a\n         <a href="/wiki/Shuttle_Carrier_Aircraft" title="Shuttle Carrier Aircraft">\n          Shuttle Carrier Aircraft\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-130_Endeavour_Rollout_6.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" </i>\n         approaches LC-39A before STS-130\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a       <i>\n          Endeavour\n         </i>\n         in flight en route back to the\n         <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n          Kennedy Space Center\n         </a>\n         atop a Shuttle Carrier Aircraft in 2008\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Space_Shuttle_Endeavour_Lands_at_the_Kennedy_Space_Center_on_July_31st,_2009..jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2008" 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Space_Shuttle_Endeavour_Lands_at_the_Kennedy_Space_Center_on_July_31st,_2009..jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <i>\n          Endeavour\n         </i>\n         lands after\n         <a href="/wiki/STS-127" title="STS-127">\n          STS-127\n         </a>\n         at the\n         <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n          Kennedy Space Center\n         </a>\n         <a href="/wiki/Shuttle_Landing_Facility" title="Shuttle Landing Facility">\n          Shuttle Landing Facility\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       As it was constructed later,\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       was built with new hardware designed to improve and expand orbiter capabilities. Most of this equipment was later incorporated into the other three orbiters during out-of-service major inspection and modification programs.\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       \xe2\x80\x99s upgrades include:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        A 40-foot (12\xc2\xa0m) diameter\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Drag_chute" title="Drag chute">\n         drag chute\n        </a>\n        that reduced the orbiter\'s\n        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Rollout_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Rollout distance (page does not exist)">\n         rollout distance\n        </a>\n        by 1,000 to 2,000 feet (300 to 610\xc2\xa0m).\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        The plumbing and electrical connections needed for\n        <a href="/wiki/Extended_Duration_Orbiter" title="Extended Duration Orbiter">\n         Extended Duration Orbiter\n        </a>\n        (EDO) modifications to allow up to a 28-day mission (although a 28-day mission was never attempted; the record is\n        <a href="/wiki/STS-80" title="STS-80">\n         17 days\n        </a>\n        , which was set by\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Columbia" title="Space Shuttle Columbia">\n          Columbia\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ).\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Updated avionics systems that included advanced\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/General_purpose_computer" title="General purpose computer">\n         general purpose computers\n        </a>\n        , improved\n        <a href="/wiki/Inertial_measurement_unit" title="Inertial measurement unit">\n         inertial measurement units\n        </a>\n        and\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tactical_air_navigation" title="Tactical air navigation">\n         tactical air navigation\n        </a>\n        systems, enhanced master events controllers and multiplexer-demultiplexers, a solid-state\n        <a href="/wiki/Star_tracker" title="Star tracker">\n         star tracker\n        </a>\n        and improved nose wheel steering mechanisms.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        An improved version of the\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Auxiliary_Power_Unit" title="Auxiliary Power Unit">\n         Auxiliary Power Units\n        </a>\n        (APUs) that provided power to operate the Shuttle\'s hydraulic systems.\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       Modifications resulting from a 2005\xe2\x80\x932006 refit of\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       included:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        The\n        <i>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Station-to-Shuttle_Power_Transfer_System" title="Station-to-Shuttle Power Transfer System">\n          Station-to-Shuttle Power Transfer System\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        (SSPTS), which converted 8 kilowatts of DC power from the ISS main voltage of 120VDC to the orbiter bus voltage of 28VDC. This upgrade allowed\n        <i>\n         Endeavour\n        </i>\n        to remain on-orbit while docked at ISS for an additional 3- to 4-day duration. The corresponding power equipment was added to the ISS during the\n        <a href="/wiki/STS-116" title="STS-116">\n         STS-116\n        </a>\n        station assembly mission, and\n        <i>\n         Endeavour\n        </i>\n        flew with SSPTS capability during\n        <a href="/wiki/STS-118" title="STS-118">\n         STS-118\n        </a>\n        .\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11">\n         <a href="#cite_note-11">\n          [11]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">\n         <a href="#cite_note-12">\n          [12]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">\n         <a href="#cite_note-13">\n          [13]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Final_flights">\n        Final flights\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Space_Shuttle_Endeavour&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Final flights">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Platforms_Around_Endeavour_In_Orbiter_Processing_Facility-2.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2008"    </i>\n         in the\n         <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Processing_Facility" title="Orbiter Processing Facility">\n          Orbiter Processing Facility\n         </a>\n         -2\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS_134_Endeavour_Docked.jpg">\n Endeavour\n         </i>\n         docked to the\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS" title="ISS">\n          ISS\n         </a>\n         for the\n         <a href="/wiki/STS-134" title="STS-134">\n          last time\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Space_Shuttle_Endeavour_over_Moffett_Field.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3456" data-file-width="5184" height="147" class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Space_Shuttle_Endeavour_over_Moffett_Field.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <i>\n          Endeavour\n         </i>\n         seen at NASA/Ames, on its final flight to California Science Center\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       flew its final mission, STS-134, to the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       (ISS) in May 2011. After the conclusion of STS-134,\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       was formally decommissioned.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14">\n        <a href="#cite_note-14">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       STS-134 was intended to launch in late 2010, but on July 1 NASA released a statement saying the\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       mission was rescheduled for February 27, 2011.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">\n        <a href="#cite_note-15">\n         [15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       "The target dates were adjusted because critical payload hardware for STS-133 will not be ready in time to support the previously planned 16 September launch," NASA said in a statement. With the\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       launch moving to November,\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       mission "cannot fly as planned, so the next available launch window is in February 2011," NASA said, adding that the launch dates were subject to change.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">\n        <a href="#cite_note-16">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2015)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The launch was further postponed until April to avoid a scheduling conflict with a Russian supply vehicle heading for the International Space Station.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17">\n        <a href="#cite_note-17">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       STS-134 did not launch until 16 May at 08:56\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Time_Zone" title="Eastern Time Zone">\n        EDT\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">\n        <a href="#cite_note-18">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       landed at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n        Kennedy Space Center\n       </a>\n       at 06:34\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coordinated_universal_time" title="Coordinated universal time">\n        UTC\n       </a>\n       on June 1, 2011, completing its final mission.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-finallanding_19-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-finallanding-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It was the 25th night landing of a shuttle.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">\n        <a href="#cite_note-20">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">\n        <a href="#cite_note-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Over its flight career,\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       flew 122,883,151 miles and spent 299 days in space.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">\n        <a href="#cite_note-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\'s\n       </i>\n       last mission, the Russian spacecraft Soyuz TMA-20 departed from the ISS and paused at a distance of 200 meters. Italian astronaut Paolo Nespoli took a series of photographs and videos of the ISS with\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       docked.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">\n        <a href="#cite_note-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This was the second time a shuttle was photographed docked and the first time since 1996. Commander\n       <a href="/wiki/Mark_Kelly" title="Mark Kelly">\n        Mark Kelly\n       </a>\n       was the last astronaut off\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       after the landing, and the crew stayed on the landing strip to sign autographs and pose for pictures.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2015)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       STS-134 was the penultimate space shuttle mission;\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-135" title="STS-135">\n        STS-135\n       </a>\n       was added to the schedule in January 2011, and in July\n       <i>\n        Atlantis\n       </i>\n       flew for the final time.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24">\n        <a href="#cite_note-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Decommissioning">\n        Decommissioning\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Space_Shuttle_Endeavour&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Decommissioning">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mission_26_The_Big_Endeavor.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="535" data-file-width="583" height="202" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Mission_26_The_Big_Endeavor.png/220px-Mission_26_The_Big_Endeavor.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Mission_26_The_Big_Endeavor.png/330px-Mission_26_The_Big_Endeavor.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Mission_26_The_Big_Endeavor.png/440px-Mission_26_The_Big_Endeavor.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mission_26_The_Big_Endeavor.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <i>\n          Endeavour\n         </i>\n         Mission 26 Patch\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Shuttle_Endeavour_in_front_of_Randys.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3744" data-file-width="5616" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Shuttle_Endeavour_in_front_of_Randys.JPG/220px-Shuttle_Endeavour_in_front_of_Randys.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Shuttle_Endeavour_in_front_of_Randys.JPG/330px-Shuttle_Endeavour_in_front_of_Randys.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Shuttle_Endeavour_in_front_of_Randys.JPG/440px-Shuttle_Endeavour_in_front_of_Randys.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Shuttle_Endeavour_in_front_of_Randys.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <i>\n          Endeavour\n         </i>\n         moving in front of Randy\'s Donuts prior to the Toyota pull\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Endeavour_docked_to_ISS.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="6048" data-file-width="4032" height="330" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Endeavour_docked_to_ISS.jpg/220px-Endeavour_docked_to_ISS.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Endeavour_docked_to_ISS.jpg/330px-Endeavour_docked_to_ISS.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Endeavour_docked_to_ISS.jpg/440px-Endeavour_docked_to_ISS.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Endeavour_docked_to_ISS.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <i>\n          Endeavour\n         </i>\n         docked to the\n         <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n          International Space Station\n         </a>\n         on May 23, 2011, during its final mission.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Endeavour_on_the_move.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3588" data-file-width="5256" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Endeavour_on_the_move.jpg/220px-Endeavour_on_the_move.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Endeavour_on_the_move.jpg/330px-Endeavour_on_the_move.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Endeavour_on_the_move.jpg/440px-Endeavour_on_the_move.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Endeavour_on_the_move.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <i>\n          Endeavour\n         </i>\n         moving though Los Angeles with Astronauts and Sci Center Director walking in front\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Endeavour_at_California_Science_Center.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2656" data-file-width="5408" height="108" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Endeavour_at_California_Science_Center.jpg/220px-Endeavour_at_California_Science_Center.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Endeavour_at_California_Science_Center.jpg/330px-Endeavour_at_California_Science_Center.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Endeavour_at_California_Science_Center.jpg/440px-Endeavour_at_California_Science_Center.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Endeavour_at_California_Science_Center.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <i>\n          Endeavour\n         </i>\n         on display at the California Science Center\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       After more than twenty organizations submitted proposals to NASA for the display of an orbiter, NASA announced that\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       would go to the\n       <a href="/wiki/California_Science_Center" title="California Science Center">\n        California Science Center\n       </a>\n       in Los Angeles.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-latshuttle_25-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-latshuttle-25">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">\n        <a href="#cite_note-26">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-usatodayshuttle_27-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-usatodayshuttle-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       After low level flyovers above NASA and civic landmarks across the country and in California, it was delivered to\n       <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_International_Airport" title="Los Angeles International Airport">\n        Los Angeles International Airport (LAX)\n       </a>\n       on September 21, 2012.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">\n        <a href="#cite_note-28">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The orbiter was slowly and carefully transported through the streets of Los Angeles and\n       <a href="/wiki/Inglewood,_California" title="Inglewood, California">\n        Inglewood\n       </a>\n       three weeks later, from October 11\xe2\x80\x9314 along La Tijera, Manchester, Crenshaw, and Martin Luther King, Jr. Boulevards to its final destination at the California Science Center in\n       <a href="/wiki/Exposition_Park,_Los_Angeles" title="Exposition Park, Los Angeles">\n        Exposition Park\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">\n        <a href="#cite_note-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">\n        <a href="#cite_note-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       encountered a few obstacles while transiting the streets narrowly missing telephone poles, apartment buildings and other structures. The lack of obstacles was due, in part, to the fact that over 400 old-growth shade trees had been cut down beforehand.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">\n        <a href="#cite_note-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The power had to be turned off and power carrying poles had to be removed temporarily as the orbiter crept along Manchester to Prairie Avenue then Crenshaw Boulevard. News crews lined the streets along the path with visible news personalities in the news trucks. There were several police escorts as well as considerable security helping to control the large crowds gathered.\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       was parked for a few hours at the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Great_Western_Forum" title="Great Western Forum">\n        Great Western Forum\n       </a>\n       where it was available for viewing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-casc_32-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-casc-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The journey was famous for an unmodified\n       <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Tundra" title="Toyota Tundra">\n        Toyota Tundra\n       </a>\n       pickup truck pulling the space shuttle across the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Manchester_Boulevard" title="Manchester Boulevard">\n        Manchester Boulevard\n       </a>\n       Bridge.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">\n        <a href="#cite_note-33">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The space shuttle was mainly carried by four self-propelled robotic dollies throughout the 12 mile journey. However, due to bridge weight restrictions, the space shuttle was moved onto the dolly towed by the Tundra. After it had completely crossed the bridge, the Space Shuttle was returned to the robotic dollies. The footage was later used in a commercial for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Super_Bowl_XLVII" title="Super Bowl XLVII">\n        2013 Super Bowl\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34">\n        <a href="#cite_note-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Having taken longer than expected,\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       finally reached the Science Center on October 14.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">\n        <a href="#cite_note-35">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The exhibit was opened to the public on October 30, 2012 at the temporary Samuel Oschin Space Shuttle\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       Display Pavilion of the museum.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-casc_32-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-casc-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A new addition to the Science Center, called the\n       <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Oschin" title="Samuel Oschin">\n        Samuel Oschin\n       </a>\n       Air and Space Center, is under construction as\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\'s\n       </i>\n       permanent home. Planned for a 2017 opening,\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       will be mounted vertically with an external tank and a pair of solid rocket boosters in the shuttle stack configuration. One payload door will be open to reveal a demonstration payload inside.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-casc_32-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-casc-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       After its decommissioning,\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\'s\n       </i>\n       <a href="/wiki/Canadarm" title="Canadarm">\n        Canadarm\n       </a>\n       (formally the \'Shuttle Remote Manipulator System\') was removed in order to be sent to the Canadian Space Agency\xe2\x80\x99s\n       <a href="/wiki/John_H._Chapman_Space_Centre" title="John H. Chapman Space Centre">\n        John H. Chapman Space Centre\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Longueuil" title="Longueuil">\n        Longueuil\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Quebec" title="Quebec">\n        Quebec\n       </a>\n       , a suburb of Montreal, where it was to be placed on display.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36">\n        <a href="#cite_note-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In a Canadian poll on which science or aerospace museum should be selected to display the Canadarm, originally built by\n       <a href="/wiki/Spar_Aerospace" title="Spar Aerospace">\n        SPAR Aerospace\n       </a>\n       , the Canadian Space Agency\xe2\x80\x99s headquarters placed third to last with only 35 out of 638 votes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">\n        <a href="#cite_note-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">\n        <a href="#cite_note-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\'s\n       </i>\n       Canadarm has since gone on permanent display at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Canada_Aviation_and_Space_Museum" title="Canada Aviation and Space Museum">\n        Canada Aviation and Space Museum\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Ottawa" title="Ottawa">\n        Ottawa\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">\n        <a href="#cite_note-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40">\n        <a href="#cite_note-40">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">\n        <a href="#cite_note-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In August 2015 NASA engineers went to work on removing a few of the tanks from\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       so that they may be used as storage containers for potable water on the International Space Station.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n        <a href="#cite_note-42">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Flights">\n        Flights\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Space_Shuttle_Endeavour&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Flights">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <table border="1" cellpadding="4" style="margin: 1em 1em 1em 0; background: #f9f9f9; border: 1px #aaa solid; border-collapse: collapse; font-size:   </td>\n        <td>\n         39-B\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Edwards_Air_Force_Base" title="Edwards Air Force Base">\n          Edwards Air Force Base\n         </a>\n        <td>\n         5\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         1993-12-02\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/STS-61" title="STS-61">\n          STS-61\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         39-B\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Kennedy\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         First\n         <a href="/wiki/Hubble_Space_Telescope" title="Hubble Space  1994-04-09\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/STS-59" title="STS-59">\n          STS-59\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         39-A\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Edwards\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Space_Radar_Laboratory&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Space Radar Laboratory (page does not       </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/STS-68" title="STS-68">\n          STS-68\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         39-A\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Edwards\n Thermal tiles protecting the underside of the vehicle were damaged during launch. NASA decided not to fix this damage in-flight as it was not believed to be serious enough to result in loss of vehicle or crew.   </b>\n         </center>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Flow_Directors">\n        Flow Directors\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Space_Shuttle_Endeavour&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Flow Directors">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       The Flow Director was responsible for the overall preparation of the shuttle for launch and processing it after landing, and remained permanently assigned to head the spacecraft\'s ground crew while the astronaut flight crews changed for every mission. Each shuttle\'s Flow Director was supported by a Vehicle Manager for the same spacecraft. Space shuttle\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\'\n       </i>\n       s Flow Directors were:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        01/1991 \xe2\x80\x93\xc2\xa0?:\n        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=John_J._%22Tip%22_Talone_Jr.&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title=\'John J. "Tip" Talone Jr. (page does not exist)\'>\n         John J. "Tip" Talone Jr.\n        </a>\n        (previously Flow Director for\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Discovery" title="Space Shuttle Discovery">\n          Discovery\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        )\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49">\n         <a href="#cite_note-49">\n          [49]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        08/2000 - 05/2006:\n        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Tassos_Abadiotakis&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Tassos Abadiotakis (page does not exist)">\n         Tassos Abadiotakis\n        </a>\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50">\n         <a href="#cite_note-50">\n          [50]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Until 08/2012:\n        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Dana_M._Hutcherson&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Dana M. Hutcherson (page does not exist)">\n         Dana M. Hutcherson\n        </a>\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51">\n         <a href="#cite_note-51">\n          [51]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="California_Science_Center">\n        California Science Center\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Space_Shuttle_Endeavour&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: California Science Center">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       is currently housed in the Samuel Oschin Pavilion at the\n       <a href="/wiki/California_Science_Center" title="California Science Center">\n        California Science Center\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Exposition_Park,_Los_Angeles" title="Exposition Park, Los Angeles">\n        Exposition Park\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/South_Los_Angeles" title="South Los Angeles">\n        South Los Angeles\n       </a>\n       about two miles south of\n       <a href="/wiki/Downtown_Los_Angeles" title="Downtown Los Angeles">\n        Downtown Los Angeles\n       </a>\n       . A companion exhibit, "\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       : The California Story", features images and artifacts that relate the shuttle program to\n       <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">\n        California\n       </a>\n       , where the orbiters were originally constructed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52">\n        <a href="#cite_note-52">\n         [52]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It has been planned for a new facility to be built with\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       attached to an external fuel tank and the two solid rocket boosters and raised in an upright position, as if\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       were to make one more flight.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="In_media">\n        In media\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Space_Shuttle_Endeavour&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: In media">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        In the 2003 film\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/The_Core" title="The Core">\n          The Core\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        , after a geologic catastrophe,\n        <i>\n         Endeavour\n        </i>\n        is featured (and destroyed in an\n        <a href="/wiki/Emergency_landing" title="Emergency landing">\n         emergency landing\n        </a>\n        in\n        <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">\n         Los Angeles\n        </a>\n        ) during an orbital mission.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        In the\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Stargate_SG-1" title="Stargate SG-1">\n          Stargate SG-1\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        \'s season 2\'s episode 1,\n        <i>\n         Endeavour\n        </i>\n        rescues SG-1 from orbit after the destruction of a Goa\'uld spacecraft.\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n  ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div aria-label="Portals" class="noprint portal plainlist tright" role="navigation" style="margin:0.5em 0 0.5em 1em;border:solid #aaa 1px">\n       <ul style="display:table;box-sizing:border-box;padding:0.1em;max-width:175px;background:#f9f9f9;font-size:85%;line-height:110%;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold">\n        <li
